Editing or republishing a draft must not silently change an active or completed session.\r\n4.4 Chapter\r\nSuggested fields\r\n• id\r\n• draftRevisionId or publishedVersionId\r\n• title\r\n• subtitle\r\n• description\r\n• orderIndex\r\n• coverAssetId\r\n• estimatedDuration\r\n• entryBlockId\r\n• completionBlockId\r\n\r\n===== PAGE 9 =====\r\nTALL TALE STUDIO  |  PHASE 1 CODEX IMPLEMENTATION BRIEF\r\n9\r\n• isOptional\r\n• metadata\r\n4.5 Story block\r\nEvery unit in the story timeline is a block.\r\nSuggested shared fields\r\n• id\r\n• chapterId\r\n• blockType\r\n• title\r\n• internalLabel\r\n• orderIndex\r\n• configuration JSON or typed child configuration\r\n• presentation configuration\r\n• completion configuration\r\n• nextBlockId for linear flow\r\n• createdAt\r\n• updatedAt\r\n• isEnabled\r\n• creatorNotes, private\r\nThe database may normalize block-specific fields or store versioned JSON. It cannot issue arbitrary \r\nadvancement commands.\r\nCritical invariant: No interface advances a session by directly editing the current block. Every outcome passes through the \r\nsame verification and progression services.\r\n", "type": "input_text"}]

} });\n+  if (existing) return existing;\n+  const updated = await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: session.id }, data: { currentSequence: { increment: 1 } }, select: { currentSequence: true } });\n+  return tx.taleSessionEvent.create({\n+    data: {\n+      sessionId: session.id,\n+      publishedVersionId: versionIdentity(session),\n+      blockId: input.blockId ?? null,\n+      eventType: input.eventType,\n+      sourceType: input.sourceType,\n+      sourceId: input.sourceId ?? null,\n+      idempotencyKey: input.idempotencyKey,\n+      payload: JSON.stringify(input.payload ?? {}),\n+      sequence: updated.currentSequence,\n+      correlationId: input.correlationId,\n+      verificationRequestId: input.verificationRequestId,\n+    },\n+  });\n+}\n+\n+async function createRequestForBlock(tx: Prisma.TransactionClient, sessionId: string, block: PublishedBlock) {\n+  const providerType = providerForBlock(block.blockType, block.configuration);\n+  if (!providerType) return null;\n+  if (futureProviders.has(providerType)) throw new Error(`${providerType} cannot be activated until a helper provider is installed.`);\n+  const existing = await tx.taleVerificationRequest.findFirst({ where: { sessionId, blockId: block.id, status: \"PENDING\" } });\n+  if (existing) return existing;\n+  const seconds = Number(block.configuration.durationSeconds ?? 0);\n+  return tx.taleVerificationRequest.create({\n+    data: {\n+      sessionId,\n+      blockId: block.id,\n+      providerType,\n+      expiresAt: providerType === \"timer\" && seconds > 0 ? new Date(Date.now() + seconds * 1000) : null,\n+      configurationSnapshot: JSON.stringify({ ...block.configuration, acceptedAnswers: block.configuration.acceptedAnswers ?? [] }),\n+    },\n+  });\n+}\n+\n+async function enterBlock(\n+  tx: Prisma.TransactionClient,\n+  session: { id: string; publishedVersionId: string | null; draftRevisionId: string | null },\n+  snapshot: PublishedTaleSnapshot,\n+  block: PublishedBlock,\n+  sourceType: string,\n+  sourceId: string | null,\n+  correlationId: string,\n+) {\n+  const chapter = chapterFor(snapshot, block.id);\n+  await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: session.id }, data: { currentBlockId: block.id, currentChapterId: chapter?.id ?? null, lastHeartbeatAt: new Date() } });\n+  const event = await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"blockEntered\", sourceType, sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${correlationId}:enter:${block.id}`, payload: { chapterId: chapter?.id, blockType: block.blockType }, correlationId });\n+  const request = await createRequestForBlock(tx, session.id, block);\n+  if (request) await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"verificationRequested\", sourceType: \"progression\", blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${correlationId}:request:${block.id}`, payload: { providerType: request.providerType }, correlationId, verificationRequestId: request.id });\n+  return event;\n+}\n+\n+function evaluateCondition(block: PublishedBlock, variables: JsonObject, inventory: string[]) {\n+  const config = block.configuration;\n+  const name = String(config.variable ?? \"\");\n+  const actual = name.startsWith(\"artifact:\") ? inventory.includes(name.slice(9)) : variables[name];\n+  const expected = config.value;\n+  switch (config.operator) {\n+    case \"notEquals\": return actual !== expected;\n+    case \"greaterThan\": return Number(actual) > Number(expected);\n+    case \"lessThan\": return Number(actual) < Number(expected);\n+    case \"contains\": return Array.isArray(actual) ? actual.includes(expected) : String(actual ?? \"\").includes(String(expected ?? \"\"));\n+    default: return actual === expected;\n+  }\n+}\n+\n+function nextBlock(snapshot: PublishedTaleSnapshot, current: PublishedBlock, variables: JsonObject, inventory: string[], selectedTarget?: string) {\n+  const blocks = flatten(snapshot);\n+  if (selectedTarget) return blocks.find((block) => block.id === selectedTarget) ?? null;\n+  if (current.blockType === \"condition\") {\n+    const success = evaluateCondition(current, variables, inventory);\n+    const configured = String(current.configuration[success ? \"successTargetBlockId\" : \"failureTargetBlockId\"] ?? \"\");\n+    return blocks.find((block) => block.id === configured) ?? null;\n+  }\n+  const target = current.connections.find((connection) => connection.connectionType === \"DEFAULT\")?.targetBlockId ?? current.nextBlockId;\n+  return blocks.find((block) => block.id === target) ?? null;\n+}\n+\n+function applyVariable(block: PublishedBlock, variables: JsonObject) {\n+  if (block.blockType !== \"setVariable\") return variables;\n+  const result = { ...variables };\n+  const key = String(block.configuration.variable ?? \"\");\n+  const operation = String(block.configuration.operation ?? \"set\");\n+  if (!key) return result;\n+  if (operation === \"increment\") result[key] = Number(result[key] ?? 0) + Number(block.configuration.value ?? 1);\n+  else if (operation === \"decrement\") result[key] = Number(result[key] ?? 0) - Number(block.configuration.value ?? 1);\n+  else if (operation === \"toggle\") result[key] = !Boolean(result[key]);\n+  else result[key] = block.configuration.value;\n+  return result;\n+}\n+\n+async function completeAndAdvance(\n+  tx: Prisma.TransactionClient,\n+  session: { id: string; publishedVersionId: string | null; draftRevisionId: string | null; variables: string; inventory: string },\n+  snapshot: PublishedTaleSnapshot,\n+  block: PublishedBlock,\n+  sourceType: string,\n+  sourceId: string | null,\n+  idempotencyKey: string,\n+  selectedTarget?: string,\n+) {\n+  const already = await tx.taleSessionEvent.findFirst({ where: { sessionId: session.id, blockId: block.id, eventType: \"blockCompleted\" } });\n+  if (already) return already;\n+  let variables = parseJsonObject(session.variables);\n+  const inventory = parseJsonArray<string>(session.inventory);\n+  variables = applyVariable(block, variables);\n+  let nextInventory = inventory;\n+  if ([\"artifactReveal\", \"collectionUpdate\"].includes(block.blockType)) {\n+    const artifactId = String(block.configuration.artifactId ?? \"\");\n+    if (artifactId && !inventory.includes(artifactId)) {\n+      nextInventory = [...inventory, artifactId];\n+      await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"artifactGranted\", sourceType, sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `grant:${session.id}:${block.id}:${artifactId}`, payload: { artifactId }, correlationId: idempotencyKey });\n+    }\n+  }\n+  if (block.blockType === \"choice\" && selectedTarget) variables[`choice:${block.id}`] = selectedTarget;\n+  await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: session.id }, data: { variables: JSON.stringify(variables), inventory: JSON.stringify(nextInventory) } });\n+  const completed = await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"blockCompleted\", sourceType, sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${idempotencyKey}:complete`, payload: { blockType: block.blockType }, correlationId: idempotencyKey });\n+  if (block.blockType === \"chapterComplete\") await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"chapterCompleted\", sourceType, sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${idempotencyKey}:chapter`, payload: { chapterId: chapterFor(snapshot, block.id)?.id }, correlationId: idempotencyKey });\n+  if (block.blockType === \"taleComplete\") {\n+    await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: session.id }, data: { status: \"COMPLETED\", completedAt: new Date() } });\n+    await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"sessionCompleted\", sourceType, sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${idempotencyKey}:session`, payload: { taleId: snapshot.tale.id }, correlationId: idempotencyKey });\n+    return completed;\n+  }\n+  let target = nextBlock(snapshot, block, variables, nextInventory, selectedTarget);\n+  const seen = new Set<string>();\n+  while (target && [\"condition\", \"setVariable\"].includes(target.blockType) && !seen.has(target.id)) {\n+    seen.add(target.id);\n+    await enterBlock(tx, session, snapshot, target, \"progression\", null, `${idempotencyKey}:logic`);\n+    variables = applyVariable(target, variables);\n+    await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: session.id }, data: { variables: JSON.stringify(variables) } });\n+    await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"blockCompleted\", sourceType: \"progression\", blockId: target.id, idempotencyKey: `${idempotencyKey}:logic:${target.id}`, payload: { automatic: true }, correlationId: idempotencyKey });\n+    target = nextBlock(snapshot, target, variables, nextInventory);\n+  }\n+  if (!target) {\n+    await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: session.id }, data: { status: \"PAUSED\" } });\n+    await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"progressionStopped\", sourceType: \"progression\", blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${idempotencyKey}:stopped`, payload: { reason: \"No valid next connection\" }, correlationId: idempotencyKey });\n+    return completed;\n+  }\n+  await enterBlock(tx, session, snapshot, target, sourceType, sourceId, idempotencyKey);\n+  return completed;\n+}\n+\n+async function loadSessionForProgression(tx: Prisma.TransactionClient, sessionId: string) {\n+  return tx.taleSession.findUniqueOrThrow({ where: { id: sessionId }, include: { version: true } });\n+}\n+\n+function emitSession(sessionId: string, event: { id: string; eventType: string; sequence: number; createdAt: Date }) {\n+  publishTaleSessionEvent(sessionId, { id: event.id, eventType: event.eventType, sequence: event.sequence, createdAt: event.createdAt.toISOString() });\n+}\n+\n+export async function startTaleSession(taleSlug: string, ownerLabel?: string) {\n+  const tale = await db.tallTale.findFirst({ where: { slug: taleSlug, archivedAt: null, latestPublishedVersionId: { not: null }, visibility: { in: [\"PUBLIC\", \"UNLISTED\"] } }, include: { versions: { where: { isCurrent: true }, take: 1 } } });\n+  const version = tale?.versions[0];\n+  if (!tale || !version) throw new Error(\"This Tall Tale is not currently available.\");\n+  const snapshot = parsePublishedSnapshot(version.contentSnapshot);\n+  const first = flatten(snapshot)[0];\n+  if (!first) throw new Error(\"This published tale has no playable entry block.\");\n+  const token = randomBytes(32).toString(\"base64url\");\n+  const correlation = randomUUID();\n+  const result = await db.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n+    const session = await tx.taleSession.create({ data: { taleId: tale.id, publishedVersionId: version.id, ownerLabel: ownerLabel?.trim() || \"Guest crew\", accessTokenHash: hashToken(token), currentChapterId: chapterFor(snapshot, first.id)?.id, currentBlockId: first.id } });\n+    await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"sessionStarted\", sourceType: \"player\", blockId: first.id, idempotencyKey: `${correlation}:session`, payload: { taleId: tale.id, versionId: version.id }, correlationId: correlation });\n+    const event = await enterBlock(tx, session, snapshot, first, \"player\", null, correlation);\n+    return { session, event };\n+  });\n+  emitSession(result.session.id, result.event);\n+  return { sessionId: result.session.id, token, taleSlug, versionId: version.id };\n+}\n+\n+export async function startPreviewSession(taleId: string, creatorId: string, startBlockId?: string) {\n+  const studio = await getStudioTale(taleId);\n+  const snapshot = snapshotFromStudio(studio);\n+  const first = (startBlockId && findBlock(snapshot, startBlockId)) || flatten(snapshot)[0];\n+  if (!first) throw new Error(\"Add a block before starting preview mode.\");\n+  const token = randomBytes(32).toString(\"base64url\");\n+  const correlation = randomUUID();\n+  const result = await db.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n+    const session = await tx.taleSession.create({ data: { taleId, publishedVersionId: null, ownerLabel: \"Studio preview\", captainId: creatorId, accessTokenHash: hashToken(token), currentChapterId: chapterFor(snapshot, first.id)?.id, currentBlockId: first.id, previewMode: true, draftRevisionId: studio.draft.id, previewSnapshot: JSON.stringify(snapshot), expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + 4 * 60 * 60 * 1000) } });\n+    await appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"previewStarted\", sourceType: \"studio\", sourceId: creatorId, blockId: first.id, idempotencyKey: `${correlation}:session`, payload: { draftRevisionId: studio.draft.id }, correlationId: correlation });\n+    const event = await enterBlock(tx, session, snapshot, first, \"studio\", creatorId, correlation);\n+    return { session, event };\n+  });\n+  emitSession(result.session.id, result.event);\n+  return { sessionId: result.session.id, token, taleSlug: studio.tale.slug, versionId: `draft:${studio.draft.id}` };\n+}\n+\n+function sanitizeConfiguration(block: PublishedBlock) {\n+  const configuration = structuredClone(block.configuration);\n+  delete configuration.acceptedAnswers;\n+  delete configuration.captainNotes;\n+  delete configuration.captainInstruction;\n+  delete configuration.futureProviderOptions;\n+  return configuration;\n+}\n+\n+export async function getTaleSessionState(sessionId: string, token?: string, captain = false) {\n+  const session = await db.taleSession.findUniqueOrThrow({ where: { id: sessionId }, include: { version: true, verificationRequests: { where: { status: \"PENDING\" }, orderBy: { requestedAt: \"desc\" }, take: 1 }, events: { orderBy: { sequence: \"desc\" }, take: 40 } } });\n+  if (!captain && (!token || hashToken(token) !== session.accessTokenHash)) throw new Error(\"This voyage session is not available to this browser.\");\n+  if (session.expiresAt && session.expiresAt < new Date()) throw new Error(\"This preview session has expired.\");\n+  const snapshot = sessionSnapshot(session);\n+  const block = findBlock(snapshot, session.currentBlockId);\n+  const chapter = chapterFor(snapshot, session.currentBlockId);\n+  const request = session.verificationRequests[0] ?? null;\n+  return {\n+    session: { id: session.id, status: session.status, previewMode: session.previewMode, versionId: versionIdentity(session), ownerLabel: session.ownerLabel, currentSequence: session.currentSequence, startedAt: session.startedAt.toISOString(), updatedAt: session.updatedAt.toISOString(), completedAt: session.completedAt?.toISOString() ?? null },\n+    tale: snapshot.tale,\n+    chapter: chapter ? { id: chapter.id, title: chapter.title, subtitle: chapter.subtitle, orderIndex: chapter.orderIndex } : null,\n+    block: block ? { ...block, configuration: sanitizeConfiguration(block), creatorNotes: captain ? block.creatorNotes : null } : null,\n+    pendingVerification: request ? { id: request.id, providerType: request.providerType, requestedAt: request.requestedAt.toISOString(), expiresAt: request.expiresAt?.toISOString() ?? null, status: request.status } : null,\n+    inventory: parseJsonArray<string>(session.inventory),\n+    variables: captain ? parseJsonObject(session.variables) : undefined,\n+    events: session.events.map((event) => ({ id: event.id, eventType: event.eventType, sourceType: event.sourceType, blockId: event.blockId, sequence: event.sequence, payload: parseJsonObject(event.payload), createdAt: event.createdAt.toISOString() })),\n+    assets: snapshot.assets.map((asset) => ({ ...asset, url: `/api/media/${asset.id}?version=${encodeURIComponent(versionIdentity(session))}` })),\n+    chapters: captain ? snapshot.chapters.map((item) => ({ id: item.id, title: item.title, blocks: item.blocks.map((candidate) => ({ id: candidate.id, title: candidate.title, blockType: candidate.blockType })) })) : undefined,\n+  };\n+}\n+\n+function normalizeAnswer(value: string, configuration: JsonObject) {\n+  let result = configuration.normalizeWhitespace === false ? value : value.trim().replace(/\\s+/g, \" \");\n+  if (!configuration.caseSensitive) result = result.toLocaleLowerCase();\n+  return result;\n+}\n+\n+export async function interactWithTaleSession(sessionId: string, token: string, input: { action: \"continue\" | \"confirm\" | \"answer\" | \"choice\" | \"timer\"; idempotencyKey: string; answer?: string; targetBlockId?: string }) {\n+  const session = await db.taleSession.findUniqueOrThrow({ where: { id: sessionId }, include: { version: true } });\n+  if (hashToken(token) !== session.accessTokenHash) throw new Error(\"This voyage session is not available to this browser.\");\n+  if (session.status !== \"ACTIVE\") throw new Error(`This session is ${session.status.toLowerCase()}.`);\n+  const snapshot = sessionSnapshot(session);\n+  const block = findBlock(snapshot, session.currentBlockId);\n+  if (!block) throw new Error(\"The current story block is unavailable.\");\n+  const request = await db.taleVerificationRequest.findFirst({ where: { sessionId, blockId: block.id, status: \"PENDING\" }, orderBy: { requestedAt: \"desc\" } });\n+  if (input.action === \"answer\") {\n+    if (!request || request.providerType !== \"textAnswer\") throw new Error(\"This block is not awaiting a text answer.\");\n+    const configuration = parseJsonObject(request.configurationSnapshot);\n+    const submitted = normalizeAnswer(input.answer ?? \"\", configuration);\n+    const accepted = Array.isArray(configuration.acceptedAnswers) && configuration.acceptedAnswers.some((answer) => typeof answer === \"string\" && normalizeAnswer(answer, configuration) === submitted);\n+    if (!accepted) {\n+      const event = await db.$transaction(async (tx) => appendEvent(tx, session, { eventType: \"verificationRejected\", sourceType: \"player\", blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${input.idempotencyKey}:rejected`, payload: { providerType: \"textAnswer\" }, verificationRequestId: request.id }));\n+      emitSession(sessionId, event);\n+      return { accepted: false, state: await getTaleSessionState(sessionId, token) };\n+    }\n+  } else if (input.action === \"timer\") {\n+    if (!request || request.providerType !== \"timer\" || !request.expiresAt || request.expiresAt > new Date()) throw new Error(\"The configured wait is not complete.\");\n+  } else if (input.action === \"choice\") {\n+    const allowed = block.connections.some((connection) => connection.connectionType === \"CHOICE\" && connection.targetBlockId === input.targetBlockId);\n+    if (!allowed) throw new Error(\"That choice is not connected to this block.\");\n+  } else if (request && request.providerType === \"captainManual\") throw new Error(\"The Captain must resolve this verification.\");\n+  const event = await db.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n+    const current = await loadSessionForProgression(tx, sessionId);\n+    if (current.currentBlockId !== block.id) throw new Error(\"The story has already advanced.\");\n+    if (request) await tx.taleVerificationRequest.update({ where: { id: request.id }, data: { status: \"SATISFIED\", resolvedAt: new Date() } });\n+    if (request) await appendEvent(tx, current, { eventType: \"verificationSatisfied\", sourceType: \"player\", blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${input.idempotencyKey}:verified`, payload: { providerType: request.providerType }, verificationRequestId: request.id, correlationId: input.idempotencyKey });\n+    return completeAndAdvance(tx, current, snapshot, block, \"player\", null, input.idempotencyKey, input.targetBlockId);\n+  });\n+  emitSession(sessionId, event);\n+  return { accepted: true, state: await getTaleSessionState(sessionId, token) };\n+}\n+\n+export async function submitVerification(unchecked: VerificationSubmission, actor: { sourceType: string; sourceId?: string }) {\n+  const submission = verificationSubmissionSchema.parse(unchecked);\n+  const duplicate = await db.taleVerificationEvent.findUnique({ where: { idempotencyKey: submission.idempotencyKey } });\n+  if (duplicate) return { duplicate: true, accepted: duplicate.accepted, rejectionReason: duplicate.rejectionReason };\n+  const request = await db.taleVerificationRequest.findUnique({ where: { id: submission.verificationRequestId }, include: { session: { include: { version: true } } } });\n+  if (!request) throw new VerificationRejectedError(\"unknownRequest\");\n+  let rejectionReason: string | null = null;\n+  const identity = versionIdentity(request.session);\n+  if (request.sessionId !== submission.sessionId) rejectionReason = \"wrongSession\";\n+  else if (identity !== submission.publishedVersionId) rejectionReason = \"wrongVersion\";\n+  else if (request.blockId !== submission.blockId || request.session.currentBlockId !== submission.blockId) rejectionReason = \"wrongBlock\";\n+  else if (request.status !== \"PENDING\") rejectionReason = \"staleRequest\";\n+  else if (request.expiresAt && request.expiresAt < new Date()) rejectionReason = \"expiredRequest\";\n+  else if (request.providerType !== submission.providerType && actor.sourceType !== \"captainOverride\" && actor.sourceType !== \"simulator\") rejectionReason = \"wrongProvider\";\n+  if (rejectionReason) {\n+    await db.taleVerificationEvent.create({ data: { requestId: request.id, eventId: submission.eventId, idempotencyKey: submission.idempotencyKey, providerType: submission.providerType, providerInstanceId: submission.providerInstanceId, result: submission.result, confidence: submission.confidence, evidence: JSON.stringify(submission.evidence ?? {}), observedAt: new Date(submission.observedAt), accepted: false, rejectionReason } });\n+    throw new VerificationRejectedError(rejectionReason);\n+  }\n+  const snapshot = sessionSnapshot(request.session);\n+  const block = findBlock(snapshot, request.blockId);\n+  if (!block) throw new VerificationRejectedError(\"unknownBlock\");\n+  const result = await db.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n+    await tx.taleVerificationEvent.create({ data: { requestId: request.id, eventId: submission.eventId, idempotencyKey: submission.idempotencyKey, providerType: submission.providerType, providerInstanceId: submission.providerInstanceId, result: submission.result, confidence: submission.confidence, evidence: JSON.stringify(submission.evidence ?? {}), observedAt: new Date(submission.observedAt), accepted: true } });\n+    const current = await loadSessionForProgression(tx, request.sessionId);\n+    if (submission.result !== \"match\") {\n+      return appendEvent(tx, current, { eventType: submission.result === \"uncertain\" ? \"verificationUncertain\" : \"verificationRejected\", sourceType: actor.sourceType, sourceId: actor.sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${submission.idempotencyKey}:outcome`, payload: { providerType: submission.providerType, confidence: submission.confidence }, verificationRequestId: request.id, correlationId: submission.eventId });\n+    }\n+    await tx.taleVerificationRequest.update({ where: { id: request.id }, data: { status: \"SATISFIED\", resolvedAt: new Date(), satisfiedByEventId: submission.eventId } });\n+    await appendEvent(tx, current, { eventType: actor.sourceType === \"captainOverride\" ? \"captainManualUnlock\" : \"verificationSatisfied\", sourceType: actor.sourceType, sourceId: actor.sourceId, blockId: block.id, idempotencyKey: `${submission.idempotencyKey}:satisfied`, payload: { providerType: submission.providerType, confidence: submission.confidence }, verificationRequestId: request.id, correlationId: submission.eventId });\n+    return completeAndAdvance(tx, current, snapshot, block, actor.sourceType, actor.sourceId ?? null, submission.idempotencyKey);\n+  });\n+  emitSession(request.sessionId, result);\n+  return { duplicate: false, accepted: true, rejectionReason: null };\n+}\n+\n+export async function captainSessionAction(sessionId: string, actorId: string, input: { action: \"approve\" | \"reject\" | \"override\" | \"pause\" | \"resume\" | \"jump\" | \"rollback\" | \"presentation\" | \"releaseHint\"; reason?: string; targetBlockId?: string; idempotencyKey: string }) {\n+  const session = await db.taleSession.findUniqueOrThrow({ where: { id: sessionId }, include: { version: true, verificationRequests: { where: { status: \"PENDING\" }, orderBy: { requestedAt: \"desc\" }, take: 1 }, events: { where: { eventType: \"blockEntered\" }, orderBy: { sequence: \"desc\" }, take: 2 } } });\n+  const snapshot = sessionSnapshot(session);\n+  const request = session.verificationRequests[0];\n+  if ([\"approve\", \"reject\", \"override\"].includes(input.action)) {\n+    if (!request) throw new Error(\"This session has no pending verification request.\");\n+    return submitVerification({ schemaVersion: 1, eventId: randomUUID(), idempotencyKey: input.idempotencyKey, eventType: \"verification.result\", providerType: request.providerType as VerificationProviderType, providerInstanceId: `captain:${actorId}`, sessionId, publishedVersionId: versionIdentity(session), blockId: request.blockId, verificationRequestId: request.id, observedAt: new Date().toISOString(), result: input.action === \"reject\" ? \"notMatch\" : \"match\", confidence: 1, evidence: { reason: input.reason ?? \"Captain action\", override: input.action === \"override\" } }, { sourceType: input.action === \"override\" ? \"captainOverride\" : \"captainManual\", sourceId: actorId });\n+  }\n+  const event = await db.$transaction(async (tx) => {\n+    const current = await loadSessionForProgression(tx, sessionId);\n+    if (input.action === \"pause\" || input.action === \"resume\") {\n+      const status = input.action === \"pause\" ? \"PAUSED\" : \"ACTIVE\";\n+      await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: sessionId }, data: { status } });\n+      return appendEvent(tx, current, { eventType: input.action === \"pause\" ? \"sessionPaused\" : \"sessionResumed\", sourceType: \"captain\", sourceId: actorId, blockId: current.currentBlockId, idempotencyKey: input.idempotencyKey, payload: { reason: input.reason ?? null } });\n+    }\n+    if (input.action === \"presentation\" || input.action === \"releaseHint\") return appendEvent(tx, current, { eventType: input.action === \"presentation\" ? \"presentationTriggered\" : \"hintReleased\", sourceType: \"captain\", sourceId: actorId, blockId: current.currentBlockId, idempotencyKey: input.idempotencyKey, payload: { reason: input.reason ?? null } });\n+    const targetId = input.action === \"rollback\" ? session.events[1]?.blockId : input.targetBlockId;\n+    const target = findBlock(snapshot, targetId ?? null);\n+    if (!target) throw new Error(\"Choose a valid target block.\");\n+    await tx.taleVerificationRequest.updateMany({ where: { sessionId, status: \"PENDING\" }, data: { status: \"CANCELLED\", resolvedAt: new Date() } });\n+    await tx.taleSession.update({ where: { id: sessionId }, data: { status: \"ACTIVE\" } });\n+    const audit = await appendEvent(tx, current, { eventType: input.action === \"rollback\" ? \"captainRollback\" : \"captainJump\", sourceType: \"captain\", sourceId: actorId, blockId: current.currentBlockId, idempotencyKey: input.idempotencyKey, payload: { fromBlockId: current.currentBlockId, targetBlockId: target.id, reason: input.reason ?? \"No reason supplied\" } });\n+    await enterBlock(tx, current, snapshot, target, \"captain\", actorId, variables[key];\n+  const expected = config.value;\n+  if (config.operator === \"notEquals\") return actual !== expected;\n+  if (config.operator === \"greaterThan\") return Number(actual) > Number(expected);\n+  if (config.operator === \"lessThan\") return Number(actual) < Number(expected);\n+  if (config.operator === \"contains\") return Array.isArray(actual) ? actual.includes(expected) : String(actual ?? \"\").includes(String(expected ?? \"\"));\n+  return actual === expected;\n+}\n+\n+function chooseNext(snapshot: PublishedTaleSnapshot, block: PublishedBlock, variables: JsonObject, block.nextBlockId;\n+  return blocks.find((candidate) => candidate.id === target) ?? null;\n+}\n+\n+function mutateVariables(block: PublishedBlock, variables: JsonObject) {\n+  if (block.blockType !== \"setVariable\") return variables;\n+  const next = { ...variables };\n+  const key = String(block.configuration.variable ?? \"\");\n+  const operation = String(block.configuration.operation ?? \"set\");\n+  if (!key) return next;\n+  if (operation === \"increment\") next[key] = Number(next[key] ?? 0) + Number(block.configuration.value ?? 1);\n+  else if (operation === \"decrement\") next[key] = Number(next[key] ?? 0) - Number(block.configuration.value ?? 1);\n+  else if (operation === \"toggle\") next[key] = !Boolean(next[key]);\n+  else next[key] = block.configuration.value;\n+  return next;\n+}\n+\n+async function completeBlock(\n+  tx: Prisma.TransactionClient,\n+  session: { id: string; publishedVersionId: string | null; draftRevisionId: string | null; variables: string; string) {\n+  const metadata = await sharp(buffer).metadata();\n+  const definitions = [\n+    { role: \"THUMBNAIL\", width: 360, quality: 72 },\n+    { role: \"PREVIEW\", width: 960, quality: 78
